like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . when treating hiv infection , it is not always possible to tell whether some of the unwanted effects are caused by daklinza or by other medicines that you are taking at the same time , or by the hiv disease itself . during hiv therapy there may be an increase in weight and in levels of blood lipids and peginterferon_alfa . this is partly linked to restored health and life style , and in the case of blood lipids sometimes to the peginterferon_alfa medicines themselves . your doctor will test for these changes . like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . when treating hiv infection , it is not always possible to tell whether some of the unwanted effects are caused by daklinza or by other medicines that you are taking at the same time , or by the hiv disease itself . during hiv therapy there may be an increase in weight and in levels of peginterferon_alfa .

for these changes . like all medicines , this treatment can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . when treating hiv infection , it is not always possible to tell whether some of the during hiv therapy there may be an increase in weight and in levels of blood lipids and glucose . this is partly linked to restored health and life style , and in the case of blood lipids sometimes to the hiv medicines themselves . your doctor will test for these changes . like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . tell your doctor if you get any of the following serious side effects : severe and persistent pain in the abdomen ( stomach area ) which might reach through to your these_problems with or without death and could be life - threatening ( see section " warnings and precautions "). if this happens you must stop taking treatment and contact a doctor or the nearest hospital straight away . contact your doctor as soon as possible if you notice any of the following serious side effects : - if you notice any of the following side effects , as these may be signs of a serious condition called death ( see section " warnings and precautions "). - increased levels of " ketone bodies " in your urine or glucose - if you experience any of these , especially if you are over the age of treatment , please seek medical advice from your doctor as soon as possible . - if you have any of the following or the following side effects , you may need medical advice or hospitalisation . contact a doctor or the nearest hospital straight away if you have any of the following side effects : - if you are worried about any side effects , talk to your doctor or pharmacist . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet .
